<IMG SRC="g570506img001.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>AMAZON.COM ANNOUNCES SECOND QUARTER SALES UP 22% TO $15.70 BILLION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">SEATTLE&#151;(BUSINESS WIRE)&#151;July 25, 2013&#151;Amazon.com, Inc. (NASDAQ: AMZN) today announced financial results for its second quarter ended
June&nbsp;30, 2013. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating cash flow increased 41% to $4.53 billion for the trailing twelve months, compared with $3.22 billion for the
trailing twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. Free cash flow&nbsp;decreased 76% to $265 million for the trailing twelve months, compared with $1.10 billion for the trailing twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2012. Free cash flow for the trailing
twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2013 includes fourth quarter 2012 cash outflows for purchases of corporate office space and property in Seattle, Washington, of $1.4 billion. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Common shares outstanding plus shares underlying stock-based awards totaled 474&nbsp;million on June&nbsp;30, 2013, compared with 468&nbsp;million one year ago. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net sales increased 22% to $15.70 billion in the second quarter, compared with $12.83 billion in second quarter 2012. Excluding the $392 million
unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in foreign exchange rates throughout the quarter, net sales grew 25% compared with second quarter 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Operating income decreased 26% to $79 million in the second quarter, compared with $107 million in second quarter 2012. The unfavorable impact from year-over-year changes in foreign exchange rates
throughout the quarter on operating income was $18 million. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net loss was $7 million in the second quarter, or $0.02 per diluted share,
compared with net income of $7 million, or $0.01 per diluted share, in second quarter 2012. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We&#146;re so grateful to our customers for
their response to Kindle devices and our digital ecosystem. This past quarter, our top 10 selling items worldwide were all digital products &#150; Kindles, Kindle Fire HDs, accessories and digital content,&#148; said Jeff Bezos, founder and CEO of
Amazon.com. &#147;The Kindle service keeps getting better. The Kindle Store now offers millions of titles including more than 350,000 exclusives that you won&#146;t find anywhere else. Prime Instant Video has surpassed 40,000 titles, including many
premium exclusives like <I>Downton Abbey</I> and <I>Under the Dome</I>. And we&#146;ve added more than a thousand books, games, educational apps, movies and TV shows to Kindle FreeTime Unlimited, bringing together in one place all the types of
content kids and parents love.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Highlights </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amazon and Viacom Inc. announced an expanded multi-year, multi-national digital video licensing agreement to bring hundreds of TV shows and thousands
of TV episodes from Viacom to Prime Instant Video, including a collection of TV shows that customers won&#146;t find on any other digital video subscription service. Prime members now have unlimited instant streaming access to popular kids&#146;
titles such as <I>Dora the Explorer</I> and <I>SpongeBob SquarePants</I>, along with top-rated shows from MTV and COMEDY CENTRAL. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

popular TV shows to Prime Instant Video such as <I>Grimm</I>, <I>Suits</I>, <I>NOVA</I>, and <I>Masterpiece</I>. Prime Instant Video now includes more than 41,000 movies and TV episodes that are available for Prime members to watch at no additional
charge. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

security requirements and compliance mandates for running sensitive US government applications and protecting data. FedRAMP certification simplifies and speeds the ability for government agencies to evaluate and adopt AWS for a wide range of
applications and workloads. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

Reduce (EMR), and adding custom SSL certificate support for CloudFront. These enhancements give customers more granular security controls over their AWS deployments, applications and sensitive data. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

customer account. In addition, AWS lowered prices on Amazon RDS instances with On-Demand price reductions of up to 28% and Reserved Instance (RI) price reductions of up to 27%. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Financial Guidance </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following
forward-looking statements reflect Amazon.com&#146;s expectations as of July&nbsp;25, 2013, and are subject to substantial uncertainty. Our results are inherently unpredictable and may be materially affected by many factors, such as fluctuations in
foreign exchange rates, changes in global economic conditions and consumer spending, world events, the rate of growth of the Internet and online commerce and the various factors detailed below. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Third Quarter 2013 Guidance </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Net sales are expected to be between $15.45 billion and $17.15 billion, or to grow between 12% and 24% compared with third quarter 2012.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A conference call will be webcast live today at 2 p.m. PT/5 p.m. ET, and will be available for at least three months at www.amazon.com/ir. This call will
contain forward-looking statements and other material information regarding the Company&#146;s financial and operating results. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>These
forward-looking statements are inherently difficult to predict. Actual results could differ materially for a variety of reasons, including, in addition to the factors discussed above, the amount that Amazon.com invests in new business opportunities
and the timing of those investments, the mix of products sold to customers, the mix of net sales derived from products as compared with services, the extent to which we owe income taxes, competition, management of growth, potential fluctuations in
operating results, international growth and expansion, the outcomes of legal proceedings and claims, fulfillment and data center optimization, risks of inventory management, seasonality, the degree to which the Company enters into, maintains, and
develops commercial agreements, acquisitions, and strategic transactions, and risks of fulfillment throughput and productivity. Other risks and uncertainties include, among others, risks related to new products, services, and technologies, system
interruptions, government regulation and taxation, payments, and fraud. In addition, the current global economic climate amplifies many of these risks. More information about factors that potentially could affect Amazon.com&#146;s financial results
is included in Amazon.com&#146;s filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;SEC&#148;), including its most recent Annual Report on Form 10-K and subsequent filings</I>. <I> </I></FONT></P>

Earth&#146;s most customer-centric company, where customers can find and discover anything they might want to buy online, and endeavors to offer its customers the lowest possible prices. Amazon.com and other sellers offer millions of unique new,
refurbished and used items in categories such as Books; Movies, Music&nbsp;&amp; Games; Digital Downloads; Electronics&nbsp;&amp; Computers; Home&nbsp;&amp; Garden; Toys, Kids&nbsp;&amp; Baby; Grocery; Apparel, Shoes&nbsp;&amp; Jewelry;
Health&nbsp;&amp; Beauty; Sports&nbsp;&amp; Outdoors; and Tools, Auto&nbsp;&amp; Industrial. Amazon Web Services provides Amazon&#146;s developer customers with access to in-the-cloud infrastructure services based on Amazon&#146;s own back-end
technology platform, which developers can use to enable virtually any type of business. Kindle Paperwhite is the most-advanced e-reader ever constructed with 62% more pixels and 25% increased contrast, a patented built-in front light for reading in
all lighting conditions, extra-long battery life, and a thin and light design. The new latest generation Kindle, the lightest and smallest Kindle, now features new, improved fonts and faster page turns. Kindle Fire HD features a stunning custom
high-definition display, exclusive Dolby audio with dual stereo speakers, high-end, laptop-grade Wi-Fi with dual-band support, dual-antennas and MIMO for faster streaming and downloads, enough storage for HD content, and the latest generation
processor and graphics engine&#151;and it is available in two display sizes&#151;7&#148; and 8.9&#148;. The large-screen Kindle Fire HD is also available with 4G wireless, and comes with a groundbreaking $49.99 introductory 4G LTE data package. The
all-new Kindle Fire features a 20% faster processor, 40% faster performance, twice the memory, and longer battery life. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amazon and its

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Certain Definitions </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Customer Accounts </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">References to customers mean customer accounts, which are unique e-mail addresses, established either when a customer places an order or when a
customer orders from other sellers on our websites. Customer accounts exclude certain customers, including customers associated with certain of our acquisitions, Amazon Payments customers, Amazon Web Services customers, and the customers of select
companies with whom we have a technology alliance or marketing and promotional relationship. Customers are considered active when they have placed an order during the preceding twelve-month period. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Seller Accounts </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">References to sellers means seller accounts, which are established when a seller receives an order from a customer account. Sellers are considered
active when they have received an order from a customer during the preceding twelve-month period. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Registered Developers

<DOCUMENT>
<TYPE>EX-99.2
<SEQUENCE>3
<FILENAME>d570506dex992.htm
<DESCRIPTION>EX-99.2
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.2</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exhibit 99.2 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Regulation G, <I>Conditions for Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures</I>, and other SEC regulations
define and prescribe the conditions for use of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Our measure of &#147;Free cash flow&#148; meets the definition of a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure.
Free cash flow is used in addition to and in conjunction with results presented in accordance with GAAP and free cash flow should not be relied upon to the exclusion of GAAP financial measures. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow, which we reconcile to &#147;Net cash provided by (used in) operating activities,&#148; is cash flow from operations
reduced by &#147;Purchases of property and equipment, including <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">internal-use</FONT> software and website development.&#148; We use free cash flow, and ratios based on it, to conduct and evaluate our business because,
although it is similar to cash flow from operations, we believe it typically will present a more conservative measure of cash flows from operations since purchases of property and equipment, including internal-use software and website development,
are a necessary component of ongoing operations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Free cash flow has limitations due to the fact that it does not represent
the residual cash flow available for discretionary expenditures. For example, free cash flow does not incorporate the portion of payments representing principal reductions of debt, obligations related to capital leases and leases accounted for as
financing arrangements, or cash payments for business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a complement to our entire consolidated statements of cash flows. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For a quantitative reconciliation of free cash flow to the most directly comparable amounts reported in accordance with GAAP, see
&#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;8-K.</FONT> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Return on Invested Capital&#148; is a ratio based on free cash flow, and as such, is also a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure.&nbsp;Return on invested capital is
trailing twelve months free cash flow divided by average &#147;Total assets&#148; minus &#147;Current liabilities&#148; (excluding the current portion, if any, of our Long-Term Debt), over the most recent five quarter ends.&nbsp;We believe return on
invested capital is a useful measure in assessing whether we are utilizing our capital efficiently.</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As with free cash flow,
return on invested capital is used in addition to and in conjunction with results presented in accordance with GAAP and return on invested capital should not be relied upon to the exclusion of GAAP financial measures.&nbsp;We include return on
invested capital, and the denominator used to calculate it (called &#147;Invested Capital&#148;) in &#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K.</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The effect on our consolidated statements of operations from changes in exchange rates versus the U.S.&nbsp;Dollar is also a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Information regarding the effect of exchange rates, versus the U.S.&nbsp;Dollar, on our consolidated statements of operations is provided to show reported period operating results had the
exchange rates remained the same as those in effect in the comparable prior year period. We include various measures on both an as-reported basis and a basis showing the effect of changes in exchange rates versus the U.S. dollar in
&#147;Supplemental Financial Information and Business Metrics&#148; in Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K. </FONT></P>
</BODY></HTML>
